            <h1>'Ultimate squad goals': University Challenge viewers go wild for an all-female team from St Anne's Oxford who trounced the opposition by 130 POINTS</h1>      
      <ul class="mol-bullets-with-font"><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>Female alumni from St Anne’s College, Oxford featured in Christmas special </strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong> Dr Janina Ramirez, </strong><strong>Jacky Rowland and Rebecca Morelle were team members</strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>Viewers particularly impressed by Dame Marcy Archer</strong></font></li><li class=""><font style="font-size:1.4em;"><strong>Show has come under fire in past for lack of female contestants in final rounds </strong></font></li></ul><p class="author-section byline-plain">By

<a href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Siofra+Brennan+For+Mailonline" class="author" rel="nofollow">Siofra Brennan For Mailonline</a>

</p><div itemprop="articleBody"><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">The show has come under fire for a lack of female representation in the final rounds, but after yesterday's episode of University Challenge things may be set to change. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">Taking part in a special festive edition of the show, a team of female alumni from St Anne’s College, Oxford - Dame Mary Archer, Dr Janina Ramirez, Jacky Rowland and Rebecca Morelle - trounced their opponents by 130 points. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">The team looked to be having so much fun as they swept to victory that, Twitter users went wild with KateCrim22 branding the team 'ultimate squad goals'.</font></p><div class="moduleFull mol-video"><a name="video" class="namedLink"></a><div class="item">

</div>    <p class="imageCaption"></p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">And Rebecca Morelle is currently global science correspondent for BBC News.</font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">Last year's semi finalists were all men, prompting Jeremy Paxman himself to question why there were no female faces on the teams during the later stages of the competition.  </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em">Commentators have previously suggested that women are reluctant to go on the show because they fear social media backlash and commentary on their looks. </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em"> </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em"> </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em"> </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em"> </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em"></font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em"> </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em"> </font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size:1.2em"></font></p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><font style="font-size: 1.2em"> </font></p></div>

<script type="text/javascript">
    DM.later('bundle', function(){
        var n = 0;
        var taboola_every_n = 10;
        var taboola_counter = 10;

        var addTaboola = function (node){
            var id = "taboola-stream-thumbnails-" + (++n);
            var taboola_node = '<div id="' + id + '" style="min-height: 280px;"></div>';
            $(node).before(taboola_node);

            window._taboola = window._taboola || [];
            _taboola.push({
                mode: 'thumbnails-b',
                container: id,
                placement: "Stream Thumbnails " + n,
                target_type: 'mix'
            });
        };

        DM.has('infinite-list', 'InfiniteList', {
url: '/api/infinite-list.html?channelShortName=femail&pageSize=10',
            total: 7.0,
            from: 0,
            onAfterAppend: function (container){
                var items = $(container).children('div');
                if(!taboola_every_n){
                    return;
                }

                items.each(function (){
                    if (taboola_counter == 0){
                        addTaboola(this);
                        taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;
                    }
                    else {
                        taboola_counter--;
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    });
</script>
